Wuxi

New Trends in the Silk Industry

The silk industry in our region had a relatively smooth year last year. However, due to a shortage of raw materials, five or six silk factories were forced to shut down. Since the beginning of spring, in addition to the six factories operated by silk industry magnate Xue Chou Xuan, including Yongtai, Huaxin, Jinji, Yongsheng, Longchang, and Minfeng, which resumed operations on the first of this month, the remaining factories, such as Ruichang, Ruichang Yong, Runde, Hefeng, Qian Shen, Qian Tai, Housheng, Jia Tai, Guangcheng, and Youcheng, are also expected to resume operations within a few days.

Furthermore, the Xingye Silk Manufacturing Co., Ltd., organized by Xue Chou Xuan, Qian Feng, and others, aims to procure raw materials, manufacture, and promote various types of raw silk and by-products. The capital is set at one million yuan, divided into 10,000 shares, each worth one hundred yuan. The first half, 500,000 yuan, will be raised initially, and a public offering will be advertised in newspapers soon, with March 15th as the deadline for subscription. The company has also leased eight silk factories, including Yuankang, Qianyuan, Nanchang, Yuanji, Taichang, Yongyu, Zhenyuan, and Yongchang, as its operating scope for this year.

Changshu

Tragic Suicide of a Female Farmer by Slitting Her Throat

Zhang Zhu, a rural woman from Shoushan Bridge in Zhuangzhen, is 40 years old. Her husband passed away early, but according to local custom, she could be married by her younger brother-in-law, so the family was still relatively peaceful. However, due to poor harvests in recent years, income has decreased, and Zhu became depressed. Unexpectedly, last year on Lunar New Year's Eve, a fire broke out, and all the houses and belongings were destroyed. At that time, a temporary shed was built for shelter, and Zhu's life became even more difficult.

On the morning of the 3rd, after her husband Lin Lin went out, she sent her children away. Zhu then used sharp scissors to cut her own throat and committed suicide. Blood flowed everywhere, and she died shortly after being moved inside. When her husband and others returned home at noon, they were distraught, and the news quickly spread. The Ding of Chu town reported to the relevant Public Security Bureau. Subsequently, the family requested an exemption from examination. After the bureau chief confirmed that Zhu had indeed committed suicide and there were no other circumstances, the exemption was granted. He also instructed the family to arrange for burial.

Hangzhou

Three More County Farmers' Banks to be Established

The Zhejiang Construction Department stated that the various county-level agricultural financial institutions, such as farmers' banks, farmers' cooperatives, and farmers' loan offices, have reached more than 40, providing over one million yuan in loans to farmers. Rural economies have been able to circulate funds as a result. In response to the requests of cooperatives in various places, the Yongrui Pingfeng Agricultural Bank was specifically ordered to establish a water loan branch, and the Jin Yongwu Agricultural Bank to establish a cloud loan branch. The Pinghu, Haiyan, and Linhai County Farmers' Loan Offices were all reorganized and expanded into Farmers' Banks.

Ningbo

The Old Jiang Bridge to be Completed in Mid-April

The construction of the Old Jiang Bridge in this port, contracted by the Shanghai Kangyi Foreign Company and supervised by Zhu, has been underway for over a year, and most of the projects have been completed. However, last month, the cold weather hindered the laying of cement on the bridge deck, and the engineering office announced a suspension of work, which will resume once the weather warms up. Therefore, the entire project is expected to be completed in mid-April this year. In order to prepare for the opening, in addition to the funds already donated, there is still a shortfall of tens of thousands of yuan. It is planned to hold a bridge opening ceremony and sell certificates, using the proceeds to make up for the shortfall. If there is still a shortfall, fundraising will be conducted separately.

Education Broadcast Special Issue

How to Improve Students' Math Performance?

— Professor Ren Mengxian of Great China University

(Lecture given to middle school students across the country on January 14th and 16th)

How can students' math performance be improved? All those engaged in math teaching constantly have this question swirling in their minds. The aspects related to this question are numerous. Without discussing those distant and broad, more immediate factors, such as school administration, school discipline, curriculum development, class size, students' entry-level, promotion standards, learning interest, and their diligence, all have a close relationship with math performance. Merely seeking solutions within the teacher alone is impossible. However, focusing solely on the teacher's aspect, from what I know: some teachers are fresh graduates from universities, possessing excellent knowledge, but their teaching is not necessarily outstanding. Some even return from studying abroad with very profound knowledge but are unable to handle middle school teaching positions. Hence, some people say that learning and teaching are two different things, and a true scholar is not necessarily a good teacher. There are also those who have been teaching for a long time with much experience, but their students' performance remains poor or even worsens. Therefore, some say that experience is unnecessary; as long as one has learned, one can teach. Which of these two views is right? I acknowledge that teaching requires knowledge, but I do not believe that those with knowledge cannot teach. If their knowledge is sufficient to teach others, how could they not be welcomed? The so-called having knowledge but not being good at teaching is just an excuse for those who fail at teaching. I also do not believe that having knowledge alone is enough to teach, or that having experience alone is enough. Fresh graduates or those who have studied abroad, though their knowledge is profound, have not taught before or have never learned how to teach, so naturally, they cannot teach well. Old teachers relying solely on old experience without seeking new knowledge or thinking of new methods, or those who have been teaching for many years but have not paid attention to research, cannot be considered experienced. Does having methods and doing research make one an ideal teacher? That depends on their personality and spirit. Therefore, math teachers—especially those who want to improve students' performance—must pay attention to the following three things:

Three Things:

First, Substantial Cultivation. An ideal teacher must possess both academic ability and experience. How can academic ability be enriched? It can be approached from both "cultivation" and "refinement":

Cultivation. Mathematics is a discipline with theory that needs proof, methods that need practice, clear systems, and wide application. Therefore, math teachers must have:

1. Profound Theory. Although middle school teaching is limited to arithmetic, algebra, geometry, trigonometry, and analytical geometry, teachers should possess rich knowledge if they teach all subjects. Even if they only teach one or two subjects, they should have a higher level of knowledge in each. For example, if a teacher teaching algebra and trigonometry does not understand the properties of functions, how can they explain the concept of variable values, variable traces, what are real numbers, what are imaginary numbers? They will always feel unclear. If a teacher teaching geometry does not know the properties of modern geometry, they will find challenging proofs or difficult constructions thorny. Therefore, what is taught may be shallow, but what is learned must be deeper. Who says that calculus, function theory, modern algebra, and advanced geometry learned in universities are useless when teaching in middle schools!

2. Ordinary Common Knowledge. It is dangerous for a teacher's knowledge to be limited to the subject they teach. Those who teach algebra inevitably have to discuss geometry, such as the graphical solutions of equations and inequalities. Those who teach geometry inevitably have to use algebra, such as the analysis of constructions, and the limits of areas and volumes. These are natural facts. Once applied to various aspects, there is sometimes a need to discuss physics and chemistry, sometimes to discuss social sciences, and sometimes even to discuss industrial and commercial affairs. Although there is no need for specialized research, ordinary common knowledge is always necessary, especially when teaching the chapters on selection and chance in algebra, where the related matters are even more diverse, such as music, sports, and even horse racing and gambling. One must understand the rules and regulations of each, how broad is that!

3. Basic Calculation Skills. As mentioned above: The foundation of trigonometry lies in algebra and geometry, and the foundation of analytical geometry lies in algebra, geometry, and trigonometry. The foundation of any subject lies in arithmetic. Learning mathematics should be like this, and teaching mathematics should be even more so. If a teacher teaching analytical geometry is not proficient in algebraic transformations or is not skillful in using trigonometry, it will not be easy to achieve simple results regarding axis shifts and the elimination of parameters. And the last step in solving any problem is always nothing more than addition, subtraction, multiplication, and division. If the teacher's calculations with numbers are slow or often contain errors, it will be even more difficult to obtain correct solutions. How can they eliminate students' confusion and increase their interest? Therefore, teachers must have sufficient training in basic calculation skills.

4. Mastery of the Subject Taught. Any subject, even taught chapter by chapter and section by section, must be thoroughly understood by the teacher. They should have unique insights and a bird's-eye view, avoiding a piecemeal explanation of the text without any extension. For example, to find the volume of any prism, one must first calculate the triangular prism. To calculate the triangular prism, one must first investigate the parallelepiped. Any parallelepiped is equal to a right parallelepiped with the same base and height. Therefore, if the method of measuring the volume of a right parallelepiped is clear, then the volume of any prism will be clear. However, this cannot be clearly presented unless the teacher has a perspective beforehand. Another example is high school algebra textbooks, which, apart from the initial part which is a review, mostly list various methods that are hardly related to each other. The teacher should have an overview of the entire book and find ways to connect them. As for teachers who cannot explain the next section without preparing the previous section, they are naturally prone to failure.

Refinement. Even if the foundation of knowledge is deep and the usual cultivation is good, academic progress is rapid. If one cannot adapt to the times and engage in further exploration without falling behind, one will stop at a certain stage and have no possibility of upward evolution. Therefore, an ideal teacher must both teach and learn. They do not need to re-enter any school or study abroad, and they can continue to improve themselves. The method of improvement is to read new books and famous magazines. It is often seen that on a teacher's desk, apart from the current textbook and a few textbooks read during their student days, there are no other books. The equipment of their school is also very simple, so they have no reference materials for the subjects they teach. In this situation, how can they improve? Therefore, teachers should do their best to acquire new books and magazines. If necessary, they should also try to borrow them. They should read more of the publications that are directly beneficial to what they teach so that their views will not be biased in one corner. In addition, they should participate in academic groups and attend academic lectures or workshops to receive new knowledge and solve doubts. These are all good opportunities to supplement teachers' cultivation, and teachers should make full use of them.

Experience is another aspect of cultivation, but it cannot be obtained while working as a school guard or while improving oneself after serving. In other words, this kind of cultivation is not knowledge learned from books but lessons learned from actual teaching. For example, when a teacher first teaches a certain subject or chooses a certain textbook for the first time, where can the book be omitted? Where should it be supplemented? Where is it easier to proceed faster? Where is it more complicated and must be explained in detail? Nothing can be known. It must be used two or three times before one can add one's own ideas. Other similar practical problems must be repeatedly tested to find more effective examples, which teachers can encounter anytime and anywhere. However, newly graduated teachers often claim to have deep knowledge and see the subjects they teach too superficially, thinking that they can teach by slightly extracting what they have learned, not considering whether there are any practical problems, let alone how to solve them. Or there are those who have been teaching for many years, used to a few books, done hundreds of exercises, and always teach like this semester after semester. They have no new feelings about the environment and the object being taught, and they do not feel any doubt. One of these two types of teachers has no experience at all, and the other has experience but it is equivalent to nothing. Neither can improve students' performance. Therefore, an ideal teacher must attach importance to experience, and the most valuable experience is:

Objective Understanding. Teachers must have ideals about teaching methods. However, if they rely solely on subjective imagination without considering the actual situation, they may have many theories but no experience. Therefore, experience must be based on facts, that is, teaching experience should be sought from teaching itself. For example, the questions raised by students in class, the errors or misinterpretations in exercises, and the performance shown in exams can all trigger a definite reaction from the teacher, which is sufficient to prove whether the teaching is appropriate and effective. The so-called "teaching and learning enhance each other" is indeed an indelible saying!

Enlightenment After Failure. A lucky teacher may be able to do what they planned because the students are at the same level, or because the students have never paid attention to what is taught, and no matter how they are taught, they never feel any difficulty. However, problems will arise once the object changes. In fact, it is not easy to be a teacher, and mathematics teachers, in particular, are not allowed to be casual. Anyone with sufficient academic ability cannot guarantee that they will not fail, but if they are enlightened by failure and improve because of enlightenment, then more failures mean more experience, and more experience means fewer failures. The experience gained through hardship is the most reliable, intimate, and flavorful. The so-called "failure is the mother of success" is something no one can deny!

However, experience must also be able to distinguish and organize, knowing what is right and continuing it, knowing what is wrong and correcting it, otherwise, fragmented pieces, right and wrong mixed, what is the use? Therefore, if a teacher can give appropriate consideration after gaining experience, write down a few systematic experience results for their own use in the future, and also for others to refer to, then their teaching performance will surely improve day by day. A teacher who makes good use of experience in this way is both improving their cultivation and researching methods. Good and practical teaching methods are obtained in this way!

Second, Research on Methods. No one denies that elementary school teachers must have methods in teaching, but middle school teachers are different. Recently, some people have even advocated that middle school teachers do not need special training. Anyone who graduates from university can go to middle school to teach based on what they have learned. Even those who come from higher normal schools sometimes only pay attention to the teaching material and neglect the teaching method. It has been seen that teachers do not realize the reasons for their teaching failures and the reasons for students' poor performance. They often lament that their knowledge may not be inferior to others, or denounce students as unworthy of teaching, without knowing that the effectiveness of teaching, apart from the teacher's substance, depends on the method. In particular, mathematics is a subject that is generally considered difficult to learn, and students' performance cannot be improved without a teacher who has methods.

What is the content of middle school mathematics teaching methods? It cannot be described in a short time. Generally speaking, there are teaching principles, teaching procedures, and performance evaluation. Classified, there are arithmetic teaching methods, algebra teaching methods, geometry and trigonometry teaching methods, etc. All of these are matters studied in the courses taught by university education colleges or higher normal departments, and there are books to read, so I won't talk too much. I will only offer some opinions on several commonly used teaching methods and issues related to after-class handling.

Newly Appointed Ambassador to Japan, Xu Shiying, to Take Office Next Month

Attended Ambassador Arim's Tea Party Last Night, Scheduled to Go to Beijing in a Week to Seek Instructions from the Authorities

Central News Agency reports: The successor to our country's ambassador to Japan, after Jiang Zuobin was transferred back to China to head the Ministry of Interior, has been repeatedly considered by the central government. Xu Shiying, who is highly respected, was mostly favored. Xu is now preparing for departure procedures and is expected to take office next month.

Outstanding Achievements in Leading Disaster Relief Efforts. Xu has been leading national disaster relief efforts for several years. In recent years, various provinces have suffered from floods and droughts almost constantly. Therefore, Xu has been tirelessly traveling to various disaster areas to handle disaster relief matters and has made outstanding achievements. The disaster victims in various provinces have also deeply felt Xu's kindness and grace. However, due to his advanced age and declining strength, Xu felt overwhelmed by this important task and repeatedly requested the central government to resign from his position as chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee, expressing his willingness to continue speaking for the disaster victims in the private sector to complete his initial aspiration to engage in charitable work. At this time, the central government was considering candidates for the ambassador to Japan, mostly favoring Xu to take the position. President Jiang and Foreign Minister Zhang repeatedly summoned Xu to Beijing to seek his consent. In view of the importance of current Sino-Japanese relations, Xu felt duty-bound and readily agreed to take on the difficult task. It was approved yesterday at the 248th Executive Yuan meeting and formally appointed.

Staying in Shanghai for a Week Before Going to Beijing. Xu arrived in Beijing a few days ago to pay respects to key figures in the central government and completed the winding up of the Disaster Relief Committee and the Huangshan Construction Committee, which he originally chaired, in order to facilitate the handover. Xu is expected to stay in Shanghai for a week before going to Beijing to seek instructions from the authorities and complete departure procedures. Commerce and China Printing Houses to Print Unified and Reconstruction Bonds

Contract to be Signed after Procedures are Negotiated, Exchange Method to be Drafted by the Ministry of Finance. Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the total amount of the Unified Public Bonds of the 25th year of the Republic of China is 146 million yuan, and the total amount of the Reconstruction Public Bonds is 34 million yuan. The bonds will be printed by the Commercial Press and the China Book Bureau. The Commerce and China Publishing Houses have been in contact with Jiang Lufu, the director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance, to negotiate the printing procedures. After the negotiation is completed, a printing contract will be signed. It is expected that all printing will be completed by the end of March. After the printing is completed and sent to the Ministry of Finance, a notice will be issued to recall the old public bonds and exchange them for new public bonds in accordance with the regulations of A, B, C, D, and E.

Method of Exchanging Public Bonds. The method of recalling the old public bonds of A, B, C, D, and E and exchanging them for unified new public bonds has been drafted by the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance. It is heard that no matter what kind of old public bonds they are, they will be exchanged for new public bonds at the full face value. No matter what kind of old treasury bills, they will be exchanged for new public bonds according to the actual number. From now on, there will be no distinction between treasury bills and public bonds. The interest rate is 6 percent, and the principal and interest will be repaid by lottery every six months. However, the repayment of principal and interest will still be handled by the National Debt Fund Management Committee.

Securities Still Suspended Yesterday. After the Chinese Merchants' Clearing House was ordered by the Ministry of Finance to temporarily suspend trading, the date of resumption of trading must be determined by the order of the Ministry. In the future, when the Unified Public Bonds are traded, only types A, B, C, D, and E will be allowed. It is heard that futures trading will be suspended.

Gu Xinyi Discusses Shanghai Industry and Commerce

Issuing New Public Bonds Can Prevent Speculation; Cash Transactions in Various Industries Reduce Self-Risk

In recent years, due to the impact of the global economic recession, domestic industry and commerce have been in a slump. Although the authorities have tried their best to seek relief last year, it is still difficult to recover in a short time. Therefore, at the end of the year, there was no improvement in collecting accounts receivable. Therefore, various industries have agreed that starting this year, all goods will be traded mainly in cash. The Central News Agency reporter specially visited Mr. Gu Xinyi, Chairman of the Soybean and Rice Industry Association, who said as follows:

Cash Transactions Facilitate Turnover

Although this city is the center of national industry and commerce, it has been affected by the global economic recession, and various businesses have been in a slump. For the banking industry, investment in industry and commerce is very small except for foreign exchange and collateral loans, resulting in difficulties in turnover for various industries, and the scope of business has to be tightened. Starting this year, various industries have decided to trade in cash. Although this has a great impact on business development, it is a last resort to reduce their own risks.

Support the Issuance of Two New Public Bonds

The decision of the Ministry of Finance to issue the Unified and Revival Public Bonds is of great significance to the prosperity of industry and commerce. In the past, the actual interest that could be obtained from the issuance of public bonds was often more than one percent. Therefore, the general banking industry and those with financial resources were very willing to invest in public bonds, and even used public bonds for speculation. This not only affected the national wealth, but also had a profound impact on industry and commerce. The profits from investing in industry and commerce may not be as high as those from public bonds. Now, the decision to issue public bonds can enable those with financial resources to be happy to invest in industry and commerce, and the economic turnover of industry and commerce will be better than before. Therefore, industry and commerce absolutely support the Ministry of Finance's issuance of new public bonds, he said.

The Lumber and Charcoal Industry Decides: All Transactions Are in Cash

During this year's business close, the collection of store accounts in the firewood and charcoal industry has not improved. It is believed that the reason is partly due to the sluggish market and partly due to the lack of consideration by the personnel in charge, resulting in arbitrary lending. If this continues, it is feared that it will affect business. In view of this, the industry association convened a meeting of managers of various firms on the afternoon of the day before yesterday to discuss and discuss the important business guidelines for this year. As a result, the management of store accounts was taken as the starting point, and the general purpose was to sell goods to stores in cash. At the very least, all accounts must be settled uniformly at the end of each month, otherwise, transactions will be stopped immediately to restrict them. All the agreed-upon measures are as follows: 1. Starting from February of this year, all goods will be sold in cash. Those with reliable credit may be allowed to open accounts, but they must be settled at the end of each month. 2. Stores must pay in legal currency (i.e., cash). If they have reliable credit, they may pay with checks, limited to one month after the sale of goods. No long-term payments will be accepted. 3. If a store's payment is not cleared by the end of the month, transactions should be stopped immediately. If an employee of the firm (i.e., a salesman) still extends credit, the person in charge must be responsible for compensating any losses, unless permitted by the manager. 4. If a store has not cleared its payment by the end of the month, the trade association may report it to the association in writing and issue a notice so that other firms can understand the contents and pay attention. The above four items are to be notified to the trade and implemented uniformly.

The North German Company's Third Express Ship: Maiden Voyage Arrives in Shanghai

Arrived on Saturday… Anchored at Kung Ho Hsiang Wharf—Ship Name: Gneisenau—

Last year, the North German Company invested heavily in building three new giant ships to launch special express mail routes to the Far East. The first two ships that have arrived in Shanghai are the Scharnhorst and Potsdam. The third new ship, the Gneisenau, was originally scheduled to depart on December 5th last year, but was delayed by one month due to incomplete internal equipment and engineering. It was not until January 3rd of this year that it began its maiden voyage to the Far East from Bremen, Germany. Its route still goes to Hamburg, then to Antwerp in Belgium, then to Southampton in England, through Morocco, Spain, and then to Genoa, and then takes the Mediterranean route to China. This time, the maiden voyage brought 155 first-class passengers from Europe (40 to Shanghai), and the second-class cabins were also full. Yesterday, the North German Company received a telegram stating that the ship had departed from Little Luzon and would arrive in Hong Kong tonight, and would arrive in Shanghai on the 8th, still anchoring at Kung Ho Hsiang Wharf.

Ship Overview

The Gneisenau is a sister ship of the same type as the Scharnhorst and Potsdam. Its load capacity is 18,160 net tons, the ship is 652 feet long and 74 feet wide, with 152 first-class cabins and 144 second-class cabins. All the ship's engines are powered by electricity, so management, cleanliness, and hygiene are very convenient and perfect, which is a pioneering achievement in the Far East. The first-class rooms include a large dining room, social room, large living room, smoking room, wine bar, gym, women's room, chapel, etc., with magnificent and great equipment. The swimming pool is on the upper deck and can get sunlight. The layout of the second-class rooms is the same as the first-class. It can temporarily travel at 20 nautical miles per hour, and can be opened to 23 nautical miles when necessary. Shanghai to Genoa is still a 23-day sea journey.

Passenger Seats are Fully Booked

After the ship arrives in Shanghai on Saturday morning on the 8th, it should normally stay for two days for people to visit. However, because it has been delayed by two days on the way (originally scheduled to arrive on the 6th), the company may suspend the visit in order to catch up with the schedule and must sail to Yokohama and Kobe, Japan, on the 9th. Because on the 19th of this month, it must return to Germany on its maiden voyage from Shanghai, and the first and second-class passenger seats from Shanghai to Europe have long been fully booked. The good business is beyond the company's expectations, so the ticket prices have already increased. According to the company, most of the passenger seats on the Potsdam in June have been booked. After that, there will be a special express new ship sailing from Shanghai every four weeks.

Chairman Lang Pei'an, Vice Chairman Lejiaer, Committee Members Ailesi and Lafengdeng, Deputy Committee Member Di Push, Secretary Xia Cheng in attendance.

The meeting adjourned at 6:00 p.m. At 8:00 p.m., Chu hosted a banquet for the Sino-Belgian delegations and all members at his residence. The Chinese delegation's work report is appended below.

Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Committee Chinese Delegation Work Report for the 24th Year

In March of the 24th year, the association met in the capital. The delegation re-elected members in accordance with the articles of association. Each of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Internal Affairs, Ministry of Railways, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Education, and Ministry of Health sent one regular and one alternate member, with a term of five years. Chu Minyi was unanimously elected as Chairman and Zeng Zhongwu as Vice Chairman. At the same time, the Sino-Economic Education and Cultural Fund Committee and the Sino-Belgian Health Construction Fund Committee were also reorganized. Zeng Zhongwu was appointed as the convener of the Cultural Committee, and Jin Shanshan was appointed as the convener of the Health Committee. Chu Minyi and Zeng Zhongwu were elected as standing committee members. The work situation over the past year is summarized as follows: The Sino-Belgian Radium Institute was handled by the delegation with funds allocated from the Health Construction Fund. The Sino-Belgian Radium Institute has achieved results. This kind of radium medical treatment is still a pioneering effort in our country. It is the latest scientific treatment. Therefore, the delegation does not hesitate to spend huge sums of money every year to handle it. Because the previous contract with the Sacred Heart Hospital had some shortcomings, it has now been agreed by both parties to sign a new one. The personnel in charge of the hospital also resigned. Now, radium therapy experts are being hired from Belgium to come to China to achieve greater results. The University Thesis Awards: The association has discussed and decided to allocate 3,000 yuan to handle the University Thesis Awards. A trial run was held in the first phase of the 22nd year, and the results were quite good. The graduating students of various universities responded very enthusiastically. After organizing a detailed reading committee, the results were read in detail, and a total of 1,700 yuan was awarded. This year, the remaining funds will be used to continue the event. The questions have been compiled and distributed to various universities for publication. The Sino-Belgian Health Construction Fund Committee held its second meeting at the Executive Yuan on March 28th to discuss various proposals related to health. After reviewing each proposal, those that are related to the nature of Sino-Belgian industries and are permanent in nature will be subsidized. Committee Member Jin Shanshan also went to various places to accept the organs subsidized by the health fund of this association for field investigation and prepared a report to the association. The Sino-Belgian Culture and Education Fund Committee: Three-quarters of the association's funds, 3.75 million US dollars, are used for the Longhai Railway and other state-owned railways. The Central Political Conference decided to use this money as the Sino-Belgian Culture and Education Fund, with interest paid at 5%. The Ministry of Railways was also ordered by the Executive Yuan to allocate the funds. The delegation held its 13th meeting in the capital, and Committee Members Zong Jian and Duan Xipeng were entrusted to contact this matter. Committee Member now serves as Vice Minister of the Ministry of Railways. Chairman Chu and Committee Member have repeatedly contacted the matter, and Committee Member表示(biǎo shì, expresses) that they will follow the principle of the Central Political Conference resolution and make every effort to allocate the interest. Pinghan Railway Lincheng Coal Mine Debt Case: Regarding the Pinghan Railway Lincheng Coal Mine debt case, after repeated letters from the delegation, the Lincheng Coal Mine said that it was in the shutdown period and had no money to repay. The Pinghan Railway only recently allocated more than 34,000 yuan in national currency. The association has returned the bonds and made an end. The funds are still kept by Chairman Chu and Committee Member in the Central Bank. Belgian Student Affairs: The Belgian student affairs this year will still be handled in accordance with the existing regulations. The scholarship method will be used to select outstanding Belgian students and subsidize them step by step by the principals of the universities where they are studying. The two students sent from China are Fan Xi and Zhao Luanzhang from the Sino-French National Institute of Technology. Both students are the champions of the graduates of the school. A list of the Belgian students who are subsidized by the association is listed below.

Shanghai County Instructs: Reduction of Deed Tax Extended for Another Five Months

The reduction of the deed tax on fields and houses in Shanghai County, which is reduced by six percent for sales and three percent for mortgages, expires at the end of January of this year. Now, the county government has received an order from the provincial government stating that from February, the tax rate for the deed tax on fields and houses was originally intended to revert to nine percent for sales and six percent for mortgages, and no further extension would be granted. However, there were partial droughts and floods in the north and south of Jiangsu Province last year, and the autumn harvest was not satisfactory. If the reduction period is not continued, people will inevitably wait and see each other, which is contrary to the purpose of enriching taxes and caring for the people. From February to the end of June, the extension period will be extended for another five months until the end of the 24th year, etc. County Magistrate Ye yesterday instructed all district offices and township offices to widely persuade and order that all untaxed deed papers be taxed, and to notify the public for universal knowledge.

Industry Department Consults City Government for Detailed Investigation: Reasons for Delaying Company Registration

In the future, there should be no delays or discrepancies in handling cases that require approval and transfer.

The Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday received a communication No. 40003 from the Ministry of Industry, stating: "Based on the report submitted by accountant Xu Yongzuo on October 26th of the 24th year, stating that the registration cases he handled for various companies have not been approved for a long time. He earnestly requests that the approval date for company registration cases be determined to ensure the smooth implementation of government orders and benefit the merchants. Enclosed is a list of ten company registration cases that have not been approved. The Ministry believes that the company registration cases listed by the accountant were all forwarded by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. Upon investigation, there were indeed delays in the forwarding time. For example, in the case of the establishment registration of Linhua Advertising Co., Ltd., the accountant stated that he was informed on July 12th that the bureau had forwarded the case, but the case was not forwarded to the Ministry until September 12th. In the case of the establishment registration of Jishi Shenchang Clock Co., Ltd., it was stated that approval was granted for forwarding on July 31st, but it was not forwarded until October 3rd. The date when the accountant received the approval for forwarding and the date when the bureau forwarded the case to the Ministry were more than two months apart. In the case of the establishment registration of Datong Chemical Industry Factory Co., Ltd. and the capital increase registration of Shangban Zhabei Water and Electricity Co., Ltd., the accountant stated that the approval for forwarding was granted on October 12th and 16th respectively, and half a month has passed, but they have not been forwarded yet. Other cases have been delayed by one or two months before being approved and forwarded. What is the actual situation? A copy of the report has been sent to order the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to investigate each case in detail and report back, and to expedite the approval and forwarding of the cases that have not been forwarded in accordance with the law. Two months have passed, and no reply has been received, making it impossible to handle the matter. Company registration cases should be forwarded promptly after approval by the competent authority and should not be delayed. Repeated orders have been issued to comply with this requirement, but the bureau still has delays. The original complainant complained to the Ministry, and the bureau failed to comply with the order to provide reasons for the delay, which is inappropriate. A copy of the accountant's original report is enclosed to request your municipal government to verify and order the bureau to comply with the Ministry's order, provide separate replies, and strictly order that all cases that need to be approved and forwarded in the future should be handled, approved, and submitted immediately upon arrival, without any delays or discrepancies." This is a matter of official friendship.

Recent News on Disaster Relief from the China International Famine Relief Commission

The China International Famine Relief Commission, located at 505 Henan Road, has spared no effort in promoting and soliciting donations since launching its efforts to provide relief for the Jianghe River flood disaster last year. It has successively raised more than 170,000 yuan in relief funds and more than 30,000 pieces of relief clothing, all of which have been distributed to the disaster areas. Recently, it has allocated another 1,000 yuan in national currency to Pastor Ming Le Lin of the Presbyterian Church in Haizhou, Northern Jiangsu, for emergency relief, and allocated 3,000 yuan in national currency to repair the Anxi to Quanzhou highway in Fujian, providing work as relief, which is being handled by Mr. Luo Jie, the president of Xisi College in Quanzhou. According to people from the association, the disaster situation last year was extremely severe, and the disaster area was vast. Although relief efforts were carried out in many ways, the disaster victims were able to barely survive the winter. However, because their houses and seeds were completely destroyed, there were people everywhere who had no homes to return to and no land to cultivate. It is imperative to provide spring relief. It is hoped that philanthropists at home and abroad will generously donate to support this righteous cause.

The China Children's Welfare Association Accepts Disaster-Stricken Children in Yanshi County

Currently, a total of 225 disaster-stricken children have been accepted. Due to the severity of the disaster in Henan and the plight of the disaster-stricken children, the China Children's Welfare Association sent Zhao Jianchi, a staff member of the Guarantee Group, to Zhengzhou, Huaxian, Yanshi, and other places last year to inspect the situation of the disaster-stricken children. In addition to subsidizing the children's welfare homes in Zhengzhou and Huaxian to cover the cost of raising disaster-stricken children, it also raised 3,200 yuan to establish a temporary shelter for disaster-stricken children in Yanshi, with a quota of 200 children, for a period of four months, in order to seek appropriate and possible relief. It is now known that the disaster-stricken children's shelter in Yanshi began accepting children on the 16th of last month (January). Huang Zhenying, Wang Zihou, Zhang Puan, and others appointed by the Children's Welfare Association are in charge of everything in the shelter. In addition to providing the disaster-stricken children with appropriate care, they are also providing them with appropriate education. The progress is quite smooth. Currently, the shelter houses 169 boys and 56 girls, for a total of 225 children, which exceeds the original quota.

The Municipal National Goods Annual Meeting Sends Letters to Major Companies to Promote Domestic Products, Scheduled Meeting to Discuss Work Outline

The Municipal National Goods Year National Goods Movement Committee will hold its second plenary council meeting on the afternoon of the 11th of this month to discuss the work outline for this year and the plan for promoting domestic products. It has also sent letters to major department stores such as Wing On and Sincere, requesting them to instruct all store employees to vigorously promote domestic goods and display domestic product samples in the showcases to facilitate customers' selection. The details are as follows:

Letter to Various Companies to Promote Domestic Goods

The Municipal National Goods Year Committee yesterday sent letters to Wing On, Sincere, Sun Sun, The Sun, Lihua, and other department stores, stating: "To Whom It May Concern: This year's Municipal National Goods Year is a city-wide movement in Shanghai to promote domestic goods, punishing the bad and rewarding the good to develop the future of domestic goods. Your company has spared no effort in promoting domestic goods over the years. However, customers are accustomed to using foreign goods, and it is necessary to change their mentality. This can only be achieved through the efforts of store employees. The responsibility of sellers should be to correct the mentality of customers. The association has recently received reports from citizens stating that the samples displayed in the major showcases along the road by your company are still promoting imported goods. It should be known that the essence of consumerism lies in not understanding the origin of goods, and if sellers still do not regard promoting domestic goods as their duty, the crisis will be even greater. Therefore, we are writing to specifically instruct all store employees to vigorously promote domestic products from now on and correct the mentality of customers. As for the goods displayed in the showcases, please also prioritize domestic products. This matter concerns the future of domestic goods. We are writing to inform you and hope that you will handle it accordingly."

Scheduled Discussion of Work Outline

The association will hold a plenary council meeting on the 11th of this month to discuss the work outline for this year and the plan for promoting domestic goods. Yesterday, it issued a notice to the council members, requesting them to attend on time. The notice stated: "Notice: The association will hold its second council meeting at 3 PM on the 12th of this month to discuss the work outline for the 25th year and the plan for promoting domestic goods. Accordingly, we are issuing this notice, and we hope that you will attend on time to discuss the progress together. This is extremely important."

The Paint and Woodware Guild Appeals for Worker Sun Zhenhua

Sun Zhenhua (also known as Du Zai), a painter who works at Ma Xiangji Paint Shop on Jiujiang Road in the British Concession, is 31 years old and a native of Xiushui, Zhejiang. On January 20th of this year, after having dinner at the shop's New Year's Eve dinner, he left the shop to return home. While passing through Huajinli, Hu Peihuan, a student from Fudan University, was robbed of her handbag by bandits on the road and shouted for help. The painter, wearing a short coat, was mistaken for a thief by two Chinese detectives from the Central Police Station, who shot and killed him. The deceased's wife, Sun, appealed to the Municipal Paint and Woodware Guild for justice. The guild agreed to accept the case and wrote to the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of Chinese Residents in the Concessions and the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce to provide assistance to achieve the goal of punishing the murderers and providing compensation. The letters to the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of Chinese Residents in the Concessions, etc., are as follows: "Respectfully, we received a letter from Ma Xiangji Paint Shop, a member of our association, which stated: 'Sun Zhenhua (also known as Sun Du Zai), a painter at our shop, is a native of Xiushui, Zhejiang, 31 years old, and has been working at our shop for five years. On January 20th of this year (December 26th of the lunar calendar), after having the New Year's Eve dinner at the shop, he received his wages and left the shop to return home. While passing near Huajinli, bandits robbed Hu Peihuan, a student from Jiangwan Fudan University, of her handbag. Hu shouted for help, and two Chinese detectives, Nos. 164 and 2211, from the Central Police Station heard the alarm and rushed to catch the thieves. They mistakenly identified the painter Sun Zhenhua as a bandit and fired their guns, firing four shots, two of which pierced Sun's body, killing him instantly. The police then transported the body to the morgue for examination. At the time of the incident, a suspect named Ji Ziqing from Tongzhou was arrested by the police and sent to the Special Court No. 1 for trial on January 21st. The case has not yet been finalized. However, Sun Zhenhua, who had died, was shot and killed by the police. Because he was carrying nothing, it was impossible to ascertain his name and age on the spot. Sun's family (Sun's mother, Wang, and wife, Fei) came to the shop to inquire. After searching for a long time with the help of our shop, they finally got the real news on January 23rd. It was found that Sun Zhenhua was originally an apprentice at Cai Chunji Paint Shop. After graduating, he obtained a worker's license and a craft license No. 505 from the General Association of Paint Industry in June of the 15th year of the Republic of China. He has been working at our shop for five years. Because he is diligent and his skills are good, he receives a monthly salary of 24 yuan and a transportation allowance of 6 yuan. He has been living at No. 134 Shengshengli, Qianjiatang South, Huanlong Road, in the French Concession for many years. His mother, Sun Wang, is 60 years old, his wife, Sun Fei, is 28 years old, and he has two sons, Jin Gen, 9 years old, and Yin Gen, 6 years old, and a daughter named Yin Feng, who is still an infant. The entire family depends on Zhenhua's work for a living. Now, he has been unjustly killed, and the entire family is doomed. It is a pitiful and regrettable situation. Your association is a legitimate organization in our industry and should provide assistance. We ask that you seek justice for the painter and find a way to resolve the aftermath. Our shop is heartbroken and has limited ability. Therefore, we are writing to inform you of the facts and according to Sun Fei, who brought her children to the association and recounted the previous situation. After a detailed investigation by our association, the facts are as described above. Colleagues from the north and south have also come to the association, requesting the association to appeal to various public organizations for assistance in this case to achieve the goal of punishing the murderers and providing compensation to comfort the wronged soul. The association has a duty to protect its members and should appeal on their behalf. Although it is the duty of the police to catch thieves, human lives should not be treated as a game. Even if the Chinese detective mistakenly identified a passerby as a robber in the chaos, he should have fired a warning shot first in self-defense. After the first shot pierced the chest and back, how could he fire a second shot to kill him and silence him? The painter was walking on the road when he encountered the police catching thieves. He wanted to avoid them, but they mistook him for a suspect. He wanted to call for help, but bullets came immediately, taking his life on the road. The police have not investigated whether the deceased was a thief, whether he had any weapons at the time of his death, or whether the suspect Ji Ziqing had any relationship with the painter. The police ignored the family members who went to the Central Police Station to appeal for justice. They disregard Chinese lives as if they were no better than chickens and dogs. Moreover, the Chinese detective is also Chinese. We are all in danger. The deceased painter was only in his thirties, had excellent skills, and died a tragic death. He leaves behind an old mother, a young wife, and several children, all of whom are young. The family is in dire straits. The association believes that the murderers must be punished to comfort the wronged soul, and compensation must be provided to support the family. Your association is a leading organization of Chinese people in the Shanghai Concessions, helping the weak and clearing away the treacherous. We are writing to you to ask for your help in appealing to the British Municipal Council to punish the murderers and provide compensation for the painter Sun Zhenhua (also known as Sun Du Zai), who was wrongly accused of being a thief by a Chinese detective from the Central Police Station and shot to death. We also ask that you guarantee that the Chinese detectives will not repeat the same mistakes in the future, so that the deceased can have justice and the living will not be displaced. Not only will the members of the association be grateful, but all the workers in the city will also praise your virtues. We await your instructions." Addressed to the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association of Chinese Residents in the Concessions.

Shenhu Inland River Joint Operation of Double Shifts

The five shipping companies on the Shanghai-Huzhou (including Linghu New City) inland river route, including Zhao Shang, Yuantong, Lixing, Zhengchang, and Lixing, previously negotiated a joint operation through the mediation of the Shanghai Inland River Shipping Industry Association. The joint operation agreement and measures have been discussed repeatedly by the five companies and have now reached a compromise. The signing and implementation of the joint operation will take place soon. It is reported that Yuantong, Zhengchang, and Lixing, which operate on alternating days, have already implemented the joint operation on the 2nd of this month and have formed a joint office named Shenhu Line Double Shift Zhengyuanli Joint Operation Office. Once the five companies have successfully signed the agreement, a joint operation company will be formed. According to reliable sources in the inland river shipping industry, after this double shift cooperation on the Shenhu Line, the five companies' overall joint plan will be easier to implement. The current double shift three companies have stipulated that the passenger ship will depart at 11 AM every day and the cargo ship will depart at 2 PM, separating passenger and cargo transportation, making it convenient for both passengers and cargo transportation.

Gu Zhuxuan and Wang Xinggao's Two Appeals: Both Scheduled for Sentencing at 2 PM on the 11th. Wang and Gu Both Firmly Deny Any Involvement in the Murder of Jia Peng. Zhao Guangfu's Testimony is Shifty and Evasive, Claiming He Never Went to the Asia Hotel.

In the case of the assassination of Tang Jia Peng, the former manager of the Great World Amusement Park, Wang Xinggao and Gu Zhuxuan were implicated as instigators. The police successively arrested and transferred them to the Special Second Court, which sentenced them to life imprisonment and fifteen years of imprisonment, respectively. Both convicts refused to accept the verdicts and separately filed appeals to the High Third Branch Court. After repeated hearings by the High Court, the case was deemed important and complex, requiring time for investigation, and therefore had not yet concluded. It was decided to conduct the hearings for both cases on the same day, yesterday, morning and afternoon. This has already been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning around 9 AM, the High Third Branch Court, represented by acting presiding judge Sun Honglin, along with associate judges Wang Yue and Li Changnian, and clerk Wu Jiayu, convened a joint session with Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei in the First Tribunal.

Wang Xinggao's Appeal

The police department was represented by lawyer Gu Shouxi, and Wang's defense lawyers Ma Shouhua, Lin Dawen, and Wu Qilun also arrived on time. Only a few of Wang's family members and relatives were present in the audience. After the court session began, Wang Xinggao, the appellant, was ordered to come forward to state his reasons for the appeal, saying that when Tang Jia Peng was killed, he himself was working as a warden in the First Prison of Hubei Province, and was not in Shanghai, and had absolutely no involvement in instigating the murder. Because in the 17th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1928], when I was in the Investigation Team of the 26th Army in Zhabei, Zhao Guangfu, who was then called Zhao Debiao, committed a robbery, and I was ordered to arrest him, which

led to a grudge and false accusation.

He further stated that the rest of his testimony was the same as that given in the previous court hearings. Thereupon, the court ordered Zhao Guangfu to be brought to the court. According to Zhao's testimony, before the murder of Tang Jia Peng, he was met by Zhou Ermujiang at the Asia Hotel. There were many people there at that time. Zhou Ermujiang told me that there was Wang Jinkui, not Wang Xinggao. When we were preparing to accuse him (referring to Wang) in prison, three prominent lawyers, Xue Zhenyi, Zhu Jincheng, and a Mr. Shen, planned it. These three people are known as prominent lawyers, so the

planning and discussion

were very thorough. After the police received the accusation, they arrested him (referring to Wang). They (referring to Xue, Zhu, and Shen) originally wanted to extort money from him (referring to Wang), so in prison, I asked inmate Liu Guobao (who is a communist murderer and is currently appealing) to draft the accusation against Wang Xinggao. Liu refused to write it for me. In fact, Wang Xinggao and Wang Jinkui are two different people, etc. The court then ordered Liu Guobao to be brought to the court. After swearing as a witness, Liu testified that Zhao Guangfu had asked him to draft an accusation against Wang Xinggao, and he testified to me that he had a grudge against Wang Xinggao over a woman. He planned to change Wang Jinkui to Wang Xinggao, and

accuse him.

At that time, I told Zhao that I would not write it for him, etc. The court also summoned Wang Rusong, the detective in charge of this case, for questioning. Wang the detective said that in this case, there was indeed a person named Wang Jinkui. Wang the detective claimed that Zhao Guangfu had stated that Wang Jinkui was Wang Xinggao at that time. At this time, Wang Xinggao declared to the court that the case was not handled by Wang the detective, but by officer Guo Shaorong, who is present today. Guo was sent to arrest Wang Jinkui at the address, but he had already fled after hearing the news. Wang Jinkui really exists. The court then summoned Guo the detective, who claimed that he had indeed gone to arrest Wang Jinkui according to the address, but Wang Jinkui had already fled far away after hearing the news. At this point, the court considered the case

already clear

and ordered the opening of arguments. First, the prosecutor was asked to present his opinion. Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei then stated his opinion. The police department's lawyer, Gu Shouxi, argued that this case has been ongoing for over a year. The court has conducted a careful investigation and has investigated in detail Wang Xinggao's work history in Hankou. The accuser Zhao Guangfu's testimony is contradictory and evasive. He requested the presiding judge to render a verdict according to the law. Finally, the three lawyers hired by the appellant Wang Xinggao, Ma, Lin, and Wu, successively argued. The court then announced the conclusion of the arguments and scheduled the sentencing for 2 PM on the 11th. The appellants were returned to custody to await instructions. When the court adjourned, it was already 1:30 PM. As for

Gu Zhuxuan's Appeal

the court hearing was held yesterday afternoon. The police department and the court maintained the same strict security measures as before, sending detectives to patrol the area around the court and working with bailiffs to maintain order inside the court. Nearly a hundred of Gu's family members and relatives were present in the audience. At 2:40 PM, acting presiding judge Sun, along with associate judges Wang and Li, and the court clerk, convened a joint session in the First Tribunal with Chief Prosecutor Zhao to continue the hearing. The police department was represented by lawyer Yao Zhaodi. The appellant Gu Zhuxuan's defense lawyers Xue Dubi, Shan Yuhua, and Lou Ying also arrived on time. After the court session began, the court ordered to

bring Gu Zhuxuan

to the stand. Gu had a short mustache on his upper lip. First, he was asked about his age and place of birth. Gu stated that he was 51 years old, from Yancheng, Jiangsu Province, and lived in Yonghe Lane on North Xizang Road. He operated many businesses, such as glass factories, shipping companies, hotels, and theaters. The theaters have now been sold off. At this point, the court announced that the case was being reheard today and asked Gu, "You were sentenced to fifteen years of imprisonment and ten years of deprivation of civil rights by the original trial court of the Second Special District for instigating murder. Do you refuse to accept this and file an appeal?" Gu answered yes. The court ordered him to state his

reasons for appeal.

Gu claimed, "I know nothing about this case. Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Xiaosizi are extorting money from me and falsely accusing me. I have no way to defend myself, and I cannot speak out. I have never met Zhao and Zhang and do not know them. I have never been to the Asia Hotel, and I have never walked on that road. I have no grudges against Tang Jia Peng. Why would I want to ask someone to kill him? I have been in Shanghai for over thirty years and have never committed any crimes. Now I am sick, so please let my lawyers present my case." The court asked, "Do you know Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Tinggui?" Gu answered, "I have never met them." The court asked, "Do you know Wang Xinggao?" Gu answered, "Yes, he is from the same hometown." The court asked, "Do you know Wang Jinkui?" Gu answered, "No, I do not know him." The court asked, "Was it Wang Xinggao who introduced Zhao and Zhang

to you?"

Gu answered, "That is not the case." The court asked, "Is Wang Xinggao your apprentice?" Gu answered, "No, please investigate. If there is any relationship, I am willing to accept severe punishment." The court asked, "According to Zhao and Zhang, Wang Xinggao introduced them to you at the Asia Hotel." Gu answered, "I have never been to the Asia Hotel." The court asked, "According to you, why would they (referring to Zhao and Zhang) accuse you?" Gu answered, "They want to ask me for money. I am sick in the hospital. My family told me about it." I have no grudges against Tang Jia Peng. Why would I kill him?" The court asked, "When did you receive the letter from Zhao Guangfu?" Gu answered, "It was around June or July of last year.

I received several letters."

Gu answered, "I do not remember clearly. My family received them. They have now been submitted to the court." The court asked, "Did you agree to give them money?" Gu answered, "They are in prison. I do not know how to send it in." The court asked, "Who delivered Zhao Guangfu's letters to you?" Gu answered, "I was in Puji Hospital. My family received them. To avoid bothering me, they did not tell me." The court asked, "Did you see the letters?" Gu answered, "I have never seen them. My family told me about them." The court asked, "According to Zhao's letter, you would have personally agreed to give him 10,000 yuan." Gu answered, "That is not the case." The court asked, "Did you see the letter from Xue Zhenyi?" Gu answered, "My family received it. Later, a relative told me that if there was such a thing, it would be better to

spend some money

to settle it. Because there was no such thing, I ignored it." The court asked, "Who is Zheng Jian San?" Gu answered, "He is a relative." The court asked, "Did Zheng Jian San also receive a letter from Xue?" Gu answered, "I was in the hospital at that time." The court asked, "What is your relationship with Xue Zhenyi?" Gu answered, "During the January 28th Incident [Shanghai War of 1932], I ran a refugee camp, and he was in the ambulance team. I did not know him before." The court asked, "Zhao Guangfu said that you asked lawyer Zhu Dianqing to meet with him before his case was finalized." Gu answered, "That is not the case." The court asked, "Do you have a relationship with Zhu Dianqing?" Gu answered, "He is also from Yancheng. There is no relationship. Now

Zhu is in Shanghai.

You can summon him for questioning." The court asked, "How long have you known Tang Jia Peng?" Gu answered, "He has been in Shanghai for twenty or thirty years. I have known him for about seven or eight years." The court asked, "Is Tang the manager of the Great World?" Gu answered, "No, someone else is in charge. But I do not know the details." The court asked, "According to you, you have no grudges against Tang?" Gu answered, "Tang and I neither worked together nor shared wealth. How could there be any grudges?" The court asked, "Then Tang Jia Peng's sister, Tang Youmei, previously reported to the case that her brother had an accident, and that you were the one who harmed him. What is going on?" Gu answered, "Tang has a wife, brothers, and sisters. If I had killed Tang Jia Peng, they would have sued me long ago. Why would they wait until Tang Youmei saw the

news in the Evening News

before reporting it?" The court asked, "Do you know Zheng Rongsheng?" Gu answered, "I know him. He runs a fruit stall in my theater and still does today." The court asked, "When was Zheng Rongsheng killed?" Gu answered, "Yes, in the same year as Tang, before Tang died." The court asked, "Do you know who killed Zheng Rongsheng?" Gu answered, "I do not know." The court asked, "Do you know Zheng Rongsheng's wife, Chen Alin?" Gu answered, "I know her." The court asked, "After your case happened, the police received a letter saying that after Zheng Rongsheng died, you went to his house and took some money, saying it was for killing Tang Jia Peng." Gu answered, "I have never been to Zheng's house. Where he lives,

how many people are in his family,

I do not know." The court asked, "Do you still owe Zheng Rongsheng 17,000 yuan? Is that correct?" Gu answered, "This amount is the deposit for the stage in the Great Theater, deposited with me. 15,000 has already been returned. 5,000 is my promissory note, which can be verified with the bank's stub. After Zheng died, the remaining amount was withdrawn by someone else. The note was not recovered because his family said they could not find it after Zheng died." The court asked, "Did Zheng's wife come to your house after her husband died?" Gu answered, "She came. The woman just cried and wanted to continue doing business. I allowed her to." The court asked, "Did Zheng's wife ever say anything about revenge to you?" Gu answered, "She did not say anything." The court asked, "The Taoist Xu Fubao,

do you know him?

Where is he now?" Gu answered, "I know him. I do not know where he is." The court asked, "Do you also know Chou Wanrong?" Gu answered, "I know him too." The court asked, "The letter said that after you, Xu Fubao, and Chou Wanrong took the money from Zheng's house, you threatened Zheng's wife not to report it. Is this true?" Gu answered, "There is no such thing." The court asked, "You said you are sick. What kind of illness do you have?" Gu answered, "Stomach problems, frequent occurrences, feeling uncomfortable all over. I was the head of the defense regiment. At the end of March and the beginning of April last year, I went to the municipal government for a meeting and was hit by a car, injuring my brain." The court asked, "Did you go to Hangzhou last spring?" Gu answered, "I go to Hangzhou from time to time. I have not been there for a year." At this point, the court ordered to

bring Zhao Guangfu

to the stand. Gu's defense lawyer, Lawyer Xue, requested the court to allow Gu Zhuxuan to sit down while waiting for questioning because he was sick and had been standing for a long time. The court approved the request. The court said to Zhao, "Today, you are brought here as a witness for Gu Zhuxuan's case. You are the one who accused Gu. Your previous statements in the original trial and to the police are inconsistent. Today, you must tell the truth and speak from your conscience. You cannot lie. When you killed Tang Jia Peng, was Gu Zhuxuan present?" Zhao answered, "This matter cannot

be spoken of from the conscience.

You have to ask the prison lawyer Xue Zhenyi to know the truth." The court asked, "Was Gu actually there?" Zhao answered, "He was not there at first, but he initiated it later. Everyone in the prison knows about this." The court asked, "Did Gu actually meet you at the Asia Hotel?" Zhao answered, "According to Zhou Ermujiang, he met Gu at the Asia Hotel." The court asked, "What exactly do you mean by initiating it later? Why didn't you say that Gu was there before?" Zhao answered, "I originally didn't know before, but I found out later. After the first trial, when I was asked who instigated the murder of Tang, I only said it was instigated by

Zhou Ermujiang."

The court asked, "Since you didn't know that Gu was there before, did you accuse him because of a grudge against Gu?" Zhao answered, "There is no grudge. Please summon the prison lawyer Xue Zhenyi for questioning, and you will understand." The court ordered Zhao to give a detailed account of what happened. Zhao said, "After I was sentenced to life imprisonment, Xue said to me that he had a plan and told me to say that Gu asked lawyer Zhu Dianqing to meet with me to appeal for me. Now Xue is turning against me, and I have to tell the truth. Xue told me that after Gu's matter was settled, he wanted to explain it to get out and asked me to send him a suit worth over a hundred yuan. He also said that he was Gu's apprentice because he was in trouble with the law, and Gu never came to see him, which caused

resentment and displeasure.

He came up with this method. Later, the police took Xue away and locked him up for more than ten days. He was unhappy with me and scolded me for asking him to be a witness in the police station instead of in court. Xue also told me to say that I had met Gu at the Da Jiangnan Hotel and the Asia Hotel, according to the verdict, but in fact, I never met Gu. There was also another lawyer in the prison called Zhu Jincheng, who also told me to say the same thing and asked me to send him a serge overcoat, leather shoes, and other items in the future. The rest of his answers were irrelevant and evasive." The court presented Xue Zhenyi with a note written by Zhao in pencil that

was given to Zhao to read.

The court asked, "Did you write this?" After Zhao read it, he answered, "I did not write this." The court said, "You entrusted Zhang Chenglian to give this note to Xue. The court has determined that you wrote it." Zhao still claimed that he did not write it. The court also showed Zhao a letter and asked, "You gave this letter to your family to forward. Did you write it?" After reading it, Zhao said, "I cannot write so well." The court asked, "You said Xue came up with the idea for you. According to this letter, it was your own idea." Zhao answered, "Xue said it was very good before. I don't know why he is like this now." The court asked, "According to the note, you saw

Gu's photo

in the Oriental Magazine and recognized him at first glance. Is there an Oriental Magazine in the prison?" The court asked, "On a piece of paper that the police found on you before, there were the names of Gu Zhuxuan, Gu Yuebo, Wang Xinggao, and twelve other people. Are you going to accuse all these people?" Zhao answered, "Xue Zhenyi knew them. He said to do it one by one." The court asked, "Is the person you testified about in Wang Xinggao's case also the one who came up with the idea for you?" Zhao answered, "Zhang Wenbing provided the testimony, only related to the case of accusing Wang Xinggao." The court asked, "Why didn't you mention Gu Zhuxuan in your own first trial?" Zhao answered, "We hadn't planned it yet." The court asked, "When you accused Wang Xinggao, did you already plan to

extort money

from Gu then?" Zhao answered, "Xue Zhenyi and Zhu Jincheng advocated it. The two of them even had disagreements about this matter." The court asked, "Did you come up with the idea to accuse Gu Zhuxuan yourself?" Zhao answered, "They (referring to Xue) told me to say that they first arrested him (referring to Gu) in the police station." Gu's defense lawyer asked the court to ask Zhao Guangfu if he had ever been to the Asia Hotel. The court asked Zhao, "Are you saying that you cannot speak from your conscience? You have only met Gu Dunyang, Zhang Xiaosizi, and others at the Bangbei Tigao Stove. You have never been to the Asia Hotel." At this point, Yu brought Xue Zhenyi to the stand and ordered him to swear as a witness and

tell the truth.

Xue testified that in April of last year, Zhao told me that he wanted to ask Gu Zhuxuan for some money so that he would not accuse him. Zhao also told me that he recognized Gu Zhuxuan from the Oriental Magazine. In July of last year, Zhao asked someone to bring me a note, asking me to be a witness and promising to split the money three-seven after the matter was settled. taught Zhang every day

how to accuse Gu Zhuxuan. Zhao's note was brought to me by inmate Zhang Chenglian." The court ordered Zhang Chenglian to be brought to the stand and ordered him to swear as a witness. According to Zhang's testimony, Zhao lived on the fourth floor in prison, Xue worked in the box room, and I worked as a sweeper. In July, on Sunday, Zhao was released to get a haircut and wrapped a note in a paper package and asked me to hand it over to Xue Zhenyi. I did not open it and did not know what it said." The court ordered Zhang Tinggui to be brought to the stand, ordered him to swear as a witness, and instructed Zhang, "You are sentenced to 20 years of imprisonment and are a witness. You must tell the truth. If you lie, you will

be punished."

Zhang said yes. According to Zhang's testimony, Zhao told me in prison that he had a relationship with Gu and asked me to accuse him of killing Tang Jia Peng. Wang Jinkui asked me to go. I did not see Gu at the Asia Hotel. Wang Jinkui told me that the person who just left was the fourth boss, but he did not say the last name Gu." Zhao Guangfu knew that his other name was Zhao Debiao, but he did not know him." The court also asked Gu Zhuxuan, "What do you have to say about the testimony of the people in the case?" the Asia Hotel.

Moreover, I have two bodyguards and a car when I go out. If I had, I would not be able to deny it. Please investigate carefully." At this point, the court considered the investigation to be complete and first asked the prosecutor to present his arguments, stating briefly that the handwriting of the accusation letter and the anonymous letter from a third party

were similar, which was quite suspicious. Please, the presiding judge,

render a verdict according to the law.

This City's Movement to Liberate Slave Girls: Registration to Begin Next Month. The Public Security Bureau to Complete Preparations This Month. Those Who Resist Liberation Will Be Punished According to the Law.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau has recently received instructions from the Municipal Government to prepare for the registration of slave girls in this city. The bureau believes that the liberation of orphaned and helpless girls is extremely important for international credibility, humanitarian principles, and legal norms. It is currently actively preparing for this and has ordered the director of the Relief Section, Guanzhi, to expedite the handling of this matter. According to Mr. Gu, the director of the Police Department attaches great importance to this, so all the preparatory work for this section can be completed by the end of this month, and registration can begin on the first day of next month. It is also planned to announce the investigation period to the public and to supervise the subordinate units to investigate the number of slave girls and register them in a list. The investigation period is four months and may be extended by two months if necessary. The registration method has also been determined. All those who keep slave girls during the investigation period should apply to the bureau for registration or have someone else do it on their behalf. Slave girls who have been registered will be unconditionally liberated and restored to freedom. If they are minors without a home to return to, or if their families are unable to support them after returning home, they should be sent to the city's relief home or other charitable organizations for placement. Slave girls who are sixteen years old or older and have no home to return to may be matched with a spouse with their consent. Slave girls who have been liberated and have no family or whose family location is unknown may have the head of the local relief home or other charitable organization appointed as their guardian. Those who keep slave girls beyond the prescribed deadline and do not apply for registration may be fined up to ten yuan and ordered to complete the registration. The fines from the preceding paragraph will be used to expand the funding for the city's relief homes or other charitable organizations. Those who keep slave girls who have been registered and refuse to liberate them will be sent to the city's judicial authorities for handling according to the law. Slave girls who have been liberated and are of legal age may, if both parties wish to change the relationship to employment, have their wages determined in accordance with the city's living conditions.

Reimers and Blanc's Appeal

Reimers and Blanc were convicted of embezzlement and fraud. Chief Judge Helmick of the United States Court for China sentenced them to five years and two years of imprisonment, respectively. Yesterday before noon, their lawyer, Franke Ring, declared to the court that they would appeal to the United States Court of Appeals for the Ninth Circuit and presented seven reasons for the appeal. Because the two men have been convicted, their previous bail bonds are naturally invalid. Therefore, the matter of bail is also involved. This matter will be decided by the chief judge within one or two days. It is known that the sentences of Reimers and Blanc have been suspended for two years and three years and one year, respectively.

According to the International Trade Bureau yesterday, the bureau has recently received several letters from foreign countries requesting domestically produced products. Case of Throwing a Chinese Man into the River: Two Detectives Tried Yesterday. 27 Witnesses Must Be Summoned. The Audience in the Courtroom Was Very Crowded.

Peter, the western detective of the Jiaxing Road Police Station, and Jute, the probationary detective, were accused of intentionally killing the Chinese man Ma Debiao by throwing him into the Hongkou River on December 1st of last year. Ma died in the hospital. After the initial trial by the British Consular Police Court, the case was transferred to the British Supreme Court for China for trial. Yesterday morning at 10 AM, Chief Justice Moss opened the trial. Within 20 minutes, he selected 12 jurors, including Mr. Sterling. Then, the Royal Counsel, Mr. Burraeswood, who was handling the prosecution, explained the legal definition of murder and the facts of the case to the jurors. He stated that there were a total of 27 witnesses to be summoned and listed their names. The audience in the courtroom yesterday was unusually crowded. Not only was every seat in the audience section occupied, but many people were also standing. The audience dispersed only after the court adjourned.
